***граничить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:граничить.html>грани́чить</a> (17537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граничить.html>грани́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">graníčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to border, to be contiguous</li>
<li>to adjoin, to abut, to neighbour on</li>
<li>to verge</li></ol>

***гранка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гранка.html>гра́нка</a> (29392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гранка.html>гра́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gránka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гранка.html>гра́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гранка.html>гра́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гранка.html>гра́нк</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> proof, galley proof, slip</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> galley</li></ol>

***грань.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a> (4530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">granĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*granь</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">granʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>гра́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>гра́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>гра́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face (of a polyhedron)</li>
<li>facet, side</li>
<li>border, verge, brink</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gráfik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:график.html>гра́фиков</a></b>)

***грация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грация.html>гра́ция</a> (21015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грация.html>гра́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грация.html>гра́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грация.html>гра́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грация.html>гра́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grace, gracefulness</li>
<li>long line bra, corselet</li>

***гребень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гребень.html>гре́бень</a> (5102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grebenь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰrebʰ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grab</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grasp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребень.html>гре́бень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grébenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребень.html>гре́бня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребень.html>гре́бни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребень.html>гре́бней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>comb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a bird</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crest, comb</li>
<li>hackle, hatchel</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребля.html>гре́бля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gréblja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грести.html>гре́бли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грести.html>гре́бли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гребля.html>гре́бель</a></b>)

***греза.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёза</a> (17324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">грѣза</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grěza</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grěza</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёза</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grjóza</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёзы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёзы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёз</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dream, daydream, vision
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1866</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoyevsky" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fyodor Dostoyevsky">Fyodor Dostoyevsky</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crime_and_Punishment" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Crime and Punishment">Crime and Punishment</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскольник.html>раско́льников</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неподвижный.html>неподви́жно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрываться.html>отрыва́ясь</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переходить.html>переходи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:греза.html>грёзы</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:созерцание.html>созерца́ние</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мал</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> кака́я-то <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волновать.html>волнова́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чила</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Raskólʹnikov sidél, smotrél nepodvížno, ne otryvájasʹ; myslʹ jevó perexodíla v <b>grjózy</b>, v sozercánije; on ni o čóm ne dúmal, no kakája-to toská volnovála jevó i múčila.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Raskolnikov sat there, unmoving, staring fixedly. His thought passed into <b>dreams</b>, into contemplation; he did not think about anything, but some melancholy worried and tormented him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***грезить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грезить.html>гре́зить</a> (19162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грезить.html>гре́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grézitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to dream <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:грезить.html>гре́зить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наяву.html>наяву́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grézitʹ</b> najavú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to daydream; be lost in reverie</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***греметь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:греметь.html>греме́ть</a> (3603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grьměti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греметь.html>греме́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gremétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогреметь.html>прогреме́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загреметь.html>загреме́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thunder <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a noise like thunder</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to rattle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a rattling noise</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гремучий.html>грему́чий</a> (20569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греметь.html>греме́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gremétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гремучий.html>грему́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gremúčij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:гремучий.html>грему́чее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:гремучий.html>грему́чей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thundering, explosive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гремучий.html>грему́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:газ.html>газ</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gremúčij</b> gaz</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>explosive</b> gas</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rattling
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гремучий.html>грему́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:змея.html>змея́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gremúčaja</b> zmejá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rattlesnake</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>rattling</b> snake</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***грести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грести.html>грести́</a> (9210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gretì</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dig, to scrape, to rake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грести.html>грести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to row, to scull</li>
<li>to rake</li></ol>

***греть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a> (5695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*grěti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">warm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θερμός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thermós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">warm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and possibly<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">warm</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gretʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согреть.html>согре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to heat (to cause an increase in temperature of an object or space)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>All imperfective compounds relating to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></b> are formed from <b>-грева́ть</b>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:греться.html>гре́ться</a> (8123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>гре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греться.html>гре́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согреться.html>согре́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погреться.html>погре́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреться.html>нагре́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прогре́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to warm oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:греться.html>гре́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grétʹsja</b> na sólnce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bask in the sun; sun oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согреться.html>согре́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sogrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погреться.html>погре́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pogrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to warm oneself by drinking hot liquid
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:согреться.html>согре́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sogrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become warm
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреться.html>нагре́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прогре́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">progrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***грецкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грецкий.html>гре́цкий</a> (18541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">грьчьскъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grĭčĭskŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греческий.html>гре́ческий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gréčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>грек</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grek</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
